in chess, when a king is under immediate attack by opponent's pieces\r\n- Checkmate - the situation in chess, when the player whose turn it is to move is in check and has no legal move to escape check.\r\n- Stalemate - the situation in chess, when the player whose turn it is to move has no legal move and is not in check.
